#                                      Created September 2019; conversion to ISTP/IACG CDFs via SKTEditor Feb 2000                           
#                                      Time tags in CDAWeb version were modified in March 2005 to use the CDAWeb convention                  
#                                      of having mid-average time tags rather than OMNI original convention of start-of-average              
#                                      time tags. The Modified (Level-3) High Resolution OMNI data files are made                            
#                                      in the same format as the omni files based on SWE_KP data.  There are a few                           
#                                      differences  between old and new high res. OMNI 1. In the new, modified Level-3                       
#                                      OMNI data files we used the Wind/SWE plasma definitive data rather than the                           
#                                      Wind/SWE plasma KP-despiked data. Using the definitive data give us possibility                       
#                                      to include the Alpha/Proton Density Ratio and use more accurate plasma parameters.                    
#                                       However, the time coverage in the new OMNI data was decreased by 2-10% - see                         
#                                      the data description at our FTP site at https://spdf.gsfc.nasa.gov/pub/data/omni/high_res_omni/modifie
#                                      For detail comparison 1-min. SWE definitive and cross-normalized SWE_KP data                          
#                                      sets see https://omniweb.gsfc.nasa.gov/ftpbrowser/wind_pla_def_kp_norm.html.                          
#                                       2. To keep the number of words and the records length the same as in the old                         
#                                      OMNI high resolution data set we replaced the PCN-index (word #45 ) in the                            
#                                      records with the new Alpha/Proton Density Ratio parameter.  3. The latest date                        
#                                      for these new data usually behind of the OMNI based on SWE_KP data.
